It is observed that the input resistance is hardly affected by the size of the HMS. Therefore, only varying the values of <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-70-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-793" role="math" style="width: 1.625em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.444em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.264em 1001.44em 2.526em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-794"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-795"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.444em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.126em 1000.66em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-796" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">S<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.604em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-797"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-798"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-799" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">x</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-800" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">2</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.07em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-70">S_{x2}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> can adjust the value of the input resistance. As shown in <a ref-type="fig" anchor="fig9" class="fulltext-link">Fig.Â 9(a)</a>, the input reactance of the antenna is increased when <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-71-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-801" role="math" style="width: 1.144em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.024em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.264em 1001.02em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-802"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-803"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.024em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.126em 1000.66em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-804" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">S<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.604em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-805"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-806"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-807" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">y<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.003em;"></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.397em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.27em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-71">S_{y}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> is increased from 18 to 22 mm. Contrary to <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-72-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-808" role="math" style="width: 1.144em; clip: rect(3.126em 1000.66em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-811" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">S<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.604em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-812"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-813"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-814" style="font-size: 70.7%; <p></p></div><div class="section_2" id="sec4f"><h3>F. Plane Reflector</h3><p>In the practical RFID system application (typical portal and ship application), the proposed antenna may be mounted on some sort of large plane reflector. The analysis of the effect of plane reflector on the performance of the proposed antenna is important for system engineers. Note that a square plane reflector with a dimension of <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-78-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-850" role="math" style="width: 4.868em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 4.387em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.384em 1004.39em 2.586em -999.997em); clip: rect(3.186em 1001.02em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-859" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">W<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.841em; left: 0.844em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-867"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-868"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-869" style="font-size: 70.7%; The increasing of <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-80-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-871" role="math" style="width: 1.745em; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.841em; left: 0.844em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-882"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-883"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-884" style="font-size: 70.7%; The increasing of <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-82-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-886" role="math" style="width: 2.225em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.985em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1001.99em 2.526em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-887"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-888"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.985em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.78em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-889" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">D</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.841em; left: 0.844em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-890"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-891"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-892" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">G</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-893" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">R</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.07em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-82">D_{GR}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> also causes poorer CP performance. To obtain a good CP performance <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-83-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-894" role="math" style="width: 6.369em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 5.709em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1005.59em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-895"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-896" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">(</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-897"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-898"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-899" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">A</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-900" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">R</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-901" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">&lt;</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-902" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">3</span><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-903" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">Â </span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-904"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-905"><span class="mstyle" id="MathJax-Span-906"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-907"><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-908" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">dB</span></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-909" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">)</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.27em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-83">({AR}&lt;3\ {\hbox{dB}})</script></tex-math></inline-formula>, the dimension of the reflector should be less than 1 m Ã 1 m, and the distance between the reflector and ground of the proposed antenna is less than 50 mm. In addition, the proposed antenna has a wide impedance bandwidth. The effect of plane reflector on the VSWR can be ignored. The effect of the reflector on the antenna gain and radiation pattern is well known. Thus, it is not given here for conciseness.</p></div><div class="section_2" id="sec4g"><h3>G. overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.604em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1002"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1003"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1004" style="font-size: 70.7%; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.604em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1009"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1010"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1011" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">w</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.07em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-95">S_{w}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> can be decreased instead of adding the value of <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-96-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1012" role="math" style="width: 1.144em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.024em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.264em 1001.02em 2.646em -999.997em); clip: rect(3.126em 1000.66em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1015" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">S<span style="display: inline-block; It is because either decreasing the value of <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-97-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1019" role="math" style="width: 1.324em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.204em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.264em 1001.2em 2.526em -999.997em); top: -2.159em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1020"><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1021"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.204em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.126em 1000.66em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1022" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">S<span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; height: 1px; width: 0.063em;"></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.604em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1023"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1024"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1025" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">w</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.165em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.07em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-97">S_{w}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> or increasing the value of <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-98-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1026" role="math" style="width: 1.144em; <div class="section" id="sec5"><div class="header article-hdr"><div class="kicker">		                        SECTION V.</div><h2>Validation in UHF RFID System</h2></div><p>To verify the operation of the proposed antenna in RFID system practical applications, the read-range measurements were carried out. In the experiment, the proposed antenna was connected with a UHF RFID reader to detect a UHF RFID tag. The maximum reliable read range was defined as the line-of-sight distance at which the reader continuously identified the tag antenna for at least 1 min. No drops to zero in the read rate (the amount of reads per second) were allowed <a ref-type="bibr" anchor="ref29" id="context_ref_29_5">[29]</a>. As we all know, the read range of passive UHF RFID systems is limited by such factors as tag characteristics and RFID reader parameters <a ref-type="bibr" anchor="ref30" id="context_ref_30_5">[30]</a>. Therefore, two different tags and the same reader were used in the experiment, which are: a Gen 2 Thin PVC tag (116306), a Gen 2 Windshield tag (116307), and a UHF Gen 2 RFID reader (216011), all made by GAO RFID Inc., Toronto, ON, Canada. The GAO's 116306 series tag, 116307 series tag, and 216011 series reader all can operate at the frequency band of 860â960 MHz. The 116306 and 116307 series tags offer read ranges of up to 3.5 and 7.0 m, respectively. In the experiment, the 216011 series reader operated at different frequency bands of 865.6â867.6, 902â928, 920.5â924.5, and 952â954 MHz with 4-W effective isotropic radiated power (EIRP). The measurement was accomplished in a spacious square at boresight and <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-99-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1033" role="math" style="width: 2.465em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.225em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1002.23em 2.405em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1034"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1035" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">Â±</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1036"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.444em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.96em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1037"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1038"><span class="mstyle" id="MathJax-Span-1039"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1040"><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-1041" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">30</span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -4.441em; left: 1.024em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1042"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1043"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1044" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">â</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.063em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.937em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-99">\pm {\hbox{30}}^{\circ}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> offset from the boresight of the antenna at all the frequency bands. The results are summarized in <a ref-type="table" anchor="table2" class="fulltext-link">TableÂ II</a>. When using the 116306 series tag, the maximum read range of 2.9â3.3 m has been obtained at boresight and 2.3â2.8 m is achieved at the directions of <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-100-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1045" role="math" style="width: 2.465em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.225em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1002.23em 2.405em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1046"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1047" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">Â±</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1048"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.444em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.96em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1049"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1050"><span class="mstyle" id="MathJax-Span-1051"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1052"><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-1053" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">30</span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -4.441em; left: 1.024em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1054"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1055"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1056" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">â</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.063em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.937em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-100">\pm {\hbox{30}}^{\circ}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> offset from the boresight. In addition, when using the 116307 series tag, the maximum read range at the directions of boresight and <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-101-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1057" role="math" style="width: 2.465em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.225em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1002.23em 2.405em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1058"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1059" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">Â±</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1060"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.444em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.186em 1000.96em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1061"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1062"><span class="mstyle" id="MathJax-Span-1063"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1064"><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-1065" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">30</span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -4.441em; left: 1.024em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1066"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1067"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1068" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">â</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.063em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.937em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-101">\pm {\hbox{30}}^{\circ}</script></tex-math></inline-formula> offset from the boresight are 6.6â7.0 and 5.5â5.8 m, respectively. The read range is comparable with that achieved by reader with single-band antennas <a ref-type="bibr" anchor="ref29" id="context_ref_29_5">[29]</a>.

<div class="section" id="sec6"><div class="header article-hdr"><div class="kicker">		                        SECTION VI.</div><h2>Conclusion</h2></div><p>In this paper, a single-fed broadband CP stacked patch antenna has been presented for universal UHF RFID applications. By means of the proposed HMS feed technique, good impedance matching and symmetrical broadside radiation patterns have been achieved. A broadband CP characteristic is obtained by selecting an optimal size of the truncated corners and using a thick air-layer substrate (about <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-102-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1069" role="math" style="width: 2.526em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 2.285em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1002.28em 2.586em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1070"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1071" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">0.1</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1072"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.024em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.126em 1000.54em 4.207em -999.997em); top: -4.021em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1073" style="font-family: MathJax_Math-italic;">Î»</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.901em; left: 0.604em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1074"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1075"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1076" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">0</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.027em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.263em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.07em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-102">0.1\lambda_{0}</script></tex-math></inline-formula>), and is slightly effected by the HMS feed structure. Thus, it is easy to design the proposed antenna. The experimental results show that the proposed antenna has an impedance bandwidth <inline-formula id=""><tex-math notation="tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-103-Frame" tabindex="0"><nobr><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1077" role="math" style="width: 7.21em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 6.489em; height: 0px; font-size: 111%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.324em 1006.37em 2.646em -999.997em); top: -2.219em; left: 0.003em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1078"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1079" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">(</span><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-1080"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1081"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1082" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">V</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1083" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">S</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1084" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">W</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1085" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">R</span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1086" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">&lt;</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1087" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.303em;">1.5</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-1088" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">)</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.225em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.33em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.27em;"></span></span></nobr></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-103">({\rm VSWR}&lt;1.5)</script></tex-math></inline-formula> of 758â983 MHz or 25.8%, a 3-dB AR bandwidth of 838â959 MHz or 13.5%, and a gain level of about 8.6 dBic or larger within the 3-dB AR bandwidth. The read-range measurements have validated that the proposed antenna can be used with the multiband RFID readers or/and readers operating at different RFID bands to achieve desired read ranges. More importantly, simple antenna structure and broadband operation property make it beneficial for RFID system configuration and implementation, as well as cost reduction. Therefore, the proposed antenna can be a good candidate for universal UHF RFID applications. In addition, a parametric study and a design guideline of the proposed antenna have been presented to provide the engineers with information for designing, modifying, and optimizing such an antenna.</p></div>
<h3>ACKNOWLEDGMENT</h3><p>The authors would like to thank F. Ma, Laird Technologies Beijing Corporation, Beijing, China, and J. Zheng, Beijing Electro-mechanical Engineering Institute, Beijing, China, for helping with the measurements. The authors would also like to thank Guest Editor of this Special Issue, K. V. S. Rao, Intermec Technologies Corporation, Everett, WA, and the reviewers for their constructive comments in improving the quality of this paper.</p></div></div>

<script>

function getCookie(name) {
	var nameEQ = name + "=";
	var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
	for(var i=0;i &lt; ca.length;i++) {
		var c = ca[i];
		while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
		if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
	}
	return null;
}

		}
	}
});

</script>

Horizontally Meandered Strip for Universal UHF RFID Applications","title":"Single-Fed Broadband Circularly Polarized Stacked Patch Antenna With Horizontally Meandered Strip for Universal UHF RFID Applications","abstract":"In this paper, a horizontally meandered strip (HMS) feed technique is proposed to achieve good impedance matching and symmetrical broadside radiation patterns for a single-fed broadband circularly polarized stacked patch antenna, which is suitable for universal ultrahigh frequency (UHF) RF identification (RFID) applications. The antenna is composed of two corner truncated patches and an HMS, all of which are printed on the upper side of the FR4 substrates. One end of the HMS is connected to the main patch by a probe, while the other end is connected to an SMA connector. Simulation results are compared with the measurements, and a good agreement is obtained. The measurements show that the antenna has an impedance bandwidth (VSWR &amp;lt;; 1.5) of about 25.8% (758-983 MHz), a 3-dB axial ratio (AR) bandwidth of about 13.5% (838-959 MHz), and a gain level of about 8.6 dBic or larger within the 3-dB AR bandwidth. Therefore, the proposed antenna can be a good candidate for universal UHF RFID readers operating at the UHF band of 840-955 MHz. In addition, a parametric study and a design guideline of the proposed antenna are presented to provide the engineers with information for designing, modifying, and optimizing such an antenna. At last, the proposed antenna is validated in RFID system applications.","keywords":[{"type":"IEEE Keywords","kwd":["Bandwidth","Feeds","Patch antennas","Antenna measurements","Radiofrequency
